                                   10752              *
                                   10753              * Niz forgot to handle the case of transparent mode I/O to
                                   10754              * the console. This occurs when commands are sent from
                                   10755              * WYLBUR to UNIX hosts (via the % or ON <hostname> commands
                                   10756              * typically). We need to translate the transparent text
                                   10757              * from ASCII to EBCDIC and handle the carriage returns and
                                   10758              * linefeed combinations. For now, we just translate all that
                                   10759              * to EBCDIC newlines, rather than trying to preserve formatting.
                                   10760              * This works for CRLF or LFCR combinations, but won't work
                                   10761              * right for just CR or LF.
                                   10762              *
